------

mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; minor-fareast;">郭丹霞、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭宏英、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭介仁</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、郭平珍、郭泉、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭秀萍</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭秀云、郭延达、郭艳华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">果然、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高兵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年生，宁夏法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年修炼法轮功。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始迫害法轮功时，他是一名高校学生，因不放弃信仰，被开除。因不放弃修炼，此前他曾被判刑两次均为<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并被拘禁在洗脑班近<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。共曾遭牢狱迫害<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日高兵又遭盐池县花马池警察抓捕，下落不明。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉，<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">高兵已遭判刑，被关押在宁夏石嘴山监狱</span>。此次高兵<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">被判刑的时间及刑期、关押到监狱的时间等情况均不详</span>。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/24/%E6%9B%BE%E9%99%B7%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-%E5%AE%81%E5%A4%8F%E7%9B%90%E6%B1%A0%E5%8E%BF%E9%AB%98%E5%85%B5%E5%86%8D%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-431827.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/24/%E6%9B%BE%E9%99%B7%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-%E5%AE%81%E5%A4%8F%E7%9B%90%E6%B1%A0%E5%8E%BF%E9%AB%98%E5%85%B5%E5%86%8D%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-431827.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高光成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东潍坊市昌乐县<span lang="EN-US">5</span>图街道办邱家河村法轮功学员。高光成曾在<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月份，因修炼法轮功被判刑十年，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年出狱。高光成在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，在昌乐县黄埠村讲法轮功时，被黄埠村周涛恶意举报，被昌乐城南派出所抓捕。城南派出所警察高玉柱带领着<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个警察强行抄家。当时因疫情期间各看守所都不收人，高玉柱从高光成手机上找到了他女儿的电话恐吓说，交<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元钱办取保候审手续，不办就送往监狱。他女儿害怕就好说歹说交了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元办理了取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，山东省潍坊市青州法院对高光成开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高恒：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，湖北省黄冈市蕲春县漕河镇上河桥村人，广东省广州市番禺区南浦岛常驻居民，基督徒，广州圣经归正教会信徒，公益人士，中国在押良心犯。因其为人正直，热心公益，笃信基督，经常自觉参与所在教会的各种事工（即服务活动），故经常受到所在教会及区域的民众好评（如<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，因广州市再次出现新管病毒升级版疫情，其所在番禺区南浦岛处于封闭管理状态，随百姓生活出现诸多不便，其所在圣经归正教会为此开展了为市民发放生活物资等活动，其一直踊跃参与其中，即是一例）；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，曾因在儿童节当天举牌呼吁“尊重生命”、“反对堕胎”，而令当局不满，次日即被广州市番禺区南浦岛警方强行要求房东对其驱离，后因其及房东持守立场，顶住压力，终未妥协；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，“六四事件”第<span lang="EN-US">32</span>周年受难者纪念日，因其在广州地铁<span lang="EN-US">2</span>号线某地铁站举牌“六月四日，为国家祷告”，并将相关图片发于网上，同时在微博上写下：“一切社会层面上的苦难，虽然往往被归结于制度与政治的丑恶，然而，究其根本，它无不源于人心中根深蒂固的罪性。就这一罪性而言，我们与屠杀的决定者、指挥者和执行者，并无根本的不同。感谢主，我们虽同为罪人，却蒙了从上帝而来的奇异恩典，悔改认罪，接受耶稣为主，从而成为上帝的儿女”等心得，很快被广东网警发现告发，遂顿遭广州当局强力打击；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日凌晨，即被广州市番禺区南浦岛派出所警方从家中抓走，自此失联；据悉，其友人称应该已被广州市公安分局警方刑事拘留，涉嫌罪名寻衅滋事。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被正式逮捕。目前被羁押广州第二看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高洪伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省东营市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，东营市东营区胜利派出所、东三路派出所、明月派出所、文汇派出所警察同时出动，商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽等法轮功学员被秘密绑架。商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽被劫持到东营市看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，东营区法院对商兆香、王子明、高宏伟、张爱丽庭审，并判处：王子明<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，商兆香<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；张爱丽<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元。四人上诉到东营市中级法院中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。高洪伟刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高洪伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日重庆<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名法轮功学员李嘉惠、张盛全、李玉华、高洪伟、秦雪美被抓捕，两年多后<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月才获悉已经被判刑。高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；张盛全、李嘉惠，被枉判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；李玉华<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高惠仙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日生，原云南省昆明钢铁公司桥钢厂职工，后被非法开除公职。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共对法轮功持续迫害中，高惠仙曾两次被中共判刑，共遭冤狱九年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日高惠仙向安宁市太平街道办事处龙箐村中共支部书记何顺贵讲法轮功真相，同时赠送了一本「明慧日历」向他祝福。结果何顺贵向公安机关诬告高惠仙。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日高惠仙正在母亲家里，被安宁市国保大队警察非法撬锁入室抓捕、抄家，警察抢走计算机、打印机、大法书籍、法轮功数据等大量私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被昆明市西山区法院判刑七年，罚款一千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: Roman&quot;;">高贤英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川泸州市合江县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十五岁。高贤英曾被非刑两次，一次<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，一次<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午，四川泸州市七名法轮功学员高贤英、董国珍、周明英、张元华、刘忠芬、帅先芳、宋平（男）驱车到泸州市合江县五通镇赶场，被派出所警察抓捕，然后带到合江九支镇派出所审问。后因年纪大，回家监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被四川泸州市合江县法院高显英被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，处罚金七千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高小娓：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西省宝鸡市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，农民，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日出生。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被宝鸡市经二路派出所绑架到宝鸡市凌云宾馆（洗脑班）至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被铐在铁椅子上<span lang="EN-US">18</span>天，臀部都坐烂了，后被关押在宝鸡市第二看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，宝鸡市金台区法院给下达起诉书及监视居住六个月通知。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被宝鸡市金台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">4000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高小雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北保定市易县裴山镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，易县城区派出所副所长靖明忠和警察刘国栋两人，跨省前往贵州省遵义市，在高小雄的打工单位，突然对他实施抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被河北涿州市法院刑庭在易县法庭通过视频庭审。近日，易县看守所打电话给高小雄的父母：高小雄被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">高永丽</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江穆棱市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，穆棱市建行小区的一位老人曹淑芳家中的玻璃碎了，法轮功学员孙士伟、高朋光、高永丽三人帮其修理。国保警察突然出现抓捕了孙士伟、高朋光、高永丽三人，并抄了三人的家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，海林市法院下判决，高永丽被诬判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，高朋光和孙士伟被诬判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，分别处以两万罚金。高永丽刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">高智晟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，陕西省榆林市佳县人，著名维权律师。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年起，开始替弱势群体维权打官司，曾处理过多宗民间维权案件；自<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年底起，开始多次上书中共当局高层，要求改变对法轮功等群体的非法处理手段，并参与对法轮功学员器官遭当局活摘指控的调查；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，与妻子公开宣布退出中国共产党；因其勇于于为当局认定的敏感性案件（注：含法轮功信仰者、地下基督教徒以及与官员发生纠纷的底层农民和私营企业家）辩护，故而曾多次受到中共官方机构或组织（<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室）黑社会手段的严重骚扰和打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其执业执照被当局吊销，随后被秘密绑架并遭到约<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月的酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被北京市第一中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日起其与外界失联，至<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月才被当局释放返京；后因其接受了美联社采访，遂被再次与外界失联，直至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其亲友才从新华社报导中得知，其缓刑已被北京法院撤销，须继续服刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日刑满出狱，此前在新疆维吾尔自治区沙雅监狱服刑。出狱后高智晟仍被严密监控，且不让治牙看病，致其因长期在狱中遭受酷刑折磨和被单独囚禁，迄今仍牙齿松动，身体健康欠佳；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其在陕北老家秘密撰写的新书《<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，起来中国》在台湾正式印刷出售，因该书涉及中共当局对其长期绑架、囚禁和施以酷刑等，以及他从信仰角度看中共<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年将会灭亡和对<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年后的中国未来宪政民主化展望等三大内容，遂令当局十分恐惧、恼怒，对其监控愈加严密。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬在老家失踪，后获知被当局控制带回北京关押。目前已遭强迫失踪<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，音信全无，生死不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">葛志慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">北京市丰台区岳各庄的维权残疾人。住北京丰台区魏家村南<span lang="EN-US">20</span>号院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号楼门<span lang="EN-US">2</span>门<span lang="EN-US">1305</span>室。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，葛志慧和同区石榴庄东街<span lang="EN-US">195</span>号的被强拆人李美青，到达中央扫黑除恶督导组驻地反映政府的黑社会化强拆，结果在督导组驻地的门口，遭到丰台区副区长带队的维稳人员的阻截，求见扫黑除恶督导组未果。但是，没隔多久，葛志慧竟遭刑事拘留。罪名是寻衅滋事。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，葛志慧被构陷案开庭，未当庭宣判。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">后葛志慧涉寻衅滋事一案于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，在北京市丰台区法院通过视频方式宣判，葛志慧被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">现被关押在丰台看守所。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/4.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/4.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">格桑梅朵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">西藏拉萨一小学女教师。格桑梅朵是第一位可以被知道的因翻墙而遭中共当局强迫失踪的藏人。据了解，格桑梅朵曾在<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>上转发外媒 《自由亚洲电台》和《挪威西藏之声》中文部有关藏区的新闻报道，以促进使用<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>的中国网友，特别是她的汉族朋友们了解西藏问题的真相。梅朵非常了解西藏的历史和现实。格桑梅朵翻墙转发外媒西藏新闻一事被发现后，当局开始对她进行迫害，她所在的小学将梅朵开除，梅朵继而于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年遭到当局强迫失踪，至今已下落不明<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。现获悉，格桑梅朵被以“泄露国家秘密”定罪，关押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">格桑秀郎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生不详，西藏那曲地区比如县达木寺僧人。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日在拉萨市被拉萨警方拘捕，后一直被秘密关押，直至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获知，其被拉萨市中级法院以“带领民众集会”罪名判处<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年有期徒刑。目前被关押在西藏拉萨的扎其监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">革命（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">他与叶尔波里（哈萨克）都是新疆伊犁州阿尔泰地区哈巴河县哈萨克族人，自由职业者，伊斯兰教信仰者，哈萨克族人权捍卫者。由于没有办理信教许可证（即未到当地政府部门申请批准），坚持自行做祷告，并经常到清真寺，因此于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5-6</span>月被抓捕，后于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬分别被阿尔泰地区哈巴河县法院以“从事非法宗教活动罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。据一位哈萨克同乡称，因他们都无正式职业，平时靠打散工或装修房子度日，二人家庭都十分贫困。被捕后，当地公安不准家属聘请律师，也拒绝向家属出示判决书。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5-6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">革振华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">63</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，黑龙江省哈尔滨市阿城区人，原阿城区低压电器厂职工，法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年曾被哈尔滨市阿城市公安局非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。在哈尔滨市长林子劳教所期间，经常遭到警察和犯人的毒打，被强迫长时间坐小板凳等。因劳教所环境恶劣，他身上长满了疥疮，疼痛难忍。每天还要强迫他做十几个小时的苦役，完不成任务就罚站。其左肋骨曾被警察和犯人打断两根，但仍不放过他，逼他出工干活，一天也不许休息。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日凌晨，他在哈尔滨市尚志市亮河镇挂条幅、散发法轮功宣传资料时，被当地警方闻讯赶来围捕、绑架，后被关押在尚志市看守所。与其一起的法轮功学员菽坤和王翠娥也遭抓捕，至今未归。因长期不知革振华的消息，其妻经多方打听，直至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月才知道丈夫革振华已被哈尔滨市尚志市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法冤判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。据悉，革振华不服，提起上诉，但二审仍维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。目前服刑地不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">根敦伦珠（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1974</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，青海藏族作家、诗人，曾是青海同仁县隆务寺僧人，过去曾数次被当局逮捕。同仁县熟悉此事的消息人士介绍，根敦伦珠对保护母语藏语文和西藏文化非常关心。他的作品在境内和流亡藏人拥有很大的影响力。根敦伦珠于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年十月在网站上发表了一首诗歌，内容是作家和艺术家需要有言论和思想不受限制的自由。尽管面临诸多限制，根敦伦珠仍坚持创作，并从其读者处获得支持。青海当局制订的藏区“扫黑除恶”政策中，把提倡“保护母语”视为黑恶势力行为。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，青海省黄南州藏族作家、诗人根敦伦珠被中共当局逮捕，关押至秘密地点，下落不明。据悉，当局在对其实施长时间监视后采取了这个行动。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">根托（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：根托，现年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">根珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：根珠，现年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿家峰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，山东省沂水县籍人，山东省淄博市桓台县马桥镇辛庄村村民，维权访民，实名举报人，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起，就开始因所在村落官员严重贪腐问题而实名举报维权，随被山东省桓台县当局视为需要打压的异己和维稳对象；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因先后三次上访投诉，被恒台县警方以“非正常上访”为由给予严厉警告；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，曾两次被恒台县警方以“非正常上访，扰乱公共场所秩序”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，又被以警方“故意损害财物”、“扬言实施放火，非法携带管制刀具”为由分别处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，曾因所在辛庄村村主任郭世勋从金城石化公司往辛庄村的西北角运输化工废渣，污染土地，而向山东省各级环保部门举报，无果后，又于次日欲往北京环保部举报，随被县政府派人拦截并遭人毒打住院；过后其虽多次继续举报违法排污的村主任郭世勋，并要求警方尽快查处打人事件和为其被殴打导致常年半头痛后遗症做鉴定，但都被拒绝；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其再次被恒台县警方抓捕刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被淄博市桓台县法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，并被要求退赔相关经济损失<span lang="EN-US">2803</span>元。出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因桓台县田庄镇文庄村的维权人士张岗遭抓捕，张岗之妹向其求助，其为营救张岗，遂不惧险境，多次向各级主管部门及新闻媒体举报、控诉恒台县公安局非法拘禁人，从而引社会热议；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，因维权者张岗已被批捕，其受张岗妹妹之托，立刻在微信群频繁发“紧急关注”，以呼吁更多正义人士关注张岗被捕事件；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，再次为声援张岗被抓事件而在新浪微博网站发文，揭露张岗所在田庄镇文庄村村委主任组织黑社会，贪污受贿、公账私存、挪用公款等渎职行为，因此文被人关注、转发近千次，遂立遭恒台县当局强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被恒台县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”等再次刑拘，随后又被恒台县检察院很快以多项罪由正式批捕，并关押于桓台县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被淄博市恒台县法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月）、“妨碍公务罪”（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月）、“敲诈勒索罪”（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月）三罪，数罪并罚决定执行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被山东省淄博市中级法院二审裁决：驳回上诉，维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US"> 2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。目前疑似在山东省淄博监狱（又称山东省第四监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿录堂：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东东营法轮功学员。耿录堂、邹佩霞老夫妻，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年已年过七旬，家住东营市胜利油田孤岛采油厂芙蓉小区。修炼大法前，夫妻俩身体很不好，耿录堂还患有高血压等疾病。一九九六年前后，老俩口修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，老俩口去河口地区赶集，向人宣传法轮功，遭人恶告，东营市河口区国保大队下属的义和镇派出所警察，于当天抓捕了夫妇俩。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开庭，后耿录堂、邹佩霞夫妇均被东营市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并被勒索罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52140367"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿潇男：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52140367;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年代出生，出版人，独立电视制作人，文化企业家，传奇天辉影视文化（北京）有限公司董事长，北京文化公共领域领军人物，公益文化思想活动策划<span lang="EN-US">/</span>执行<span lang="EN-US">/</span>传播者，中国在押政治犯。 耿潇男早年曾就读于中央戏剧学院，毕业后逐渐成为中国文化出版人，电影人，历任中国天画画天影业首席执行官、瑞雅书业总编辑，之后又和丈夫秦真共同创立传奇天辉影视文化（北京）有限公司，并担任董事长，随在业界知名度较高；近年来，因在北京文化公共领域以活跃、敢言着称，并积极致力于公益文化思想活动策划、执行及传播活动等，遂遭北京当局的维稳监控打压；<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦真<span lang="EN-US">/</span>耿潇男夫妇二人突然被警方带走，随后被北京市海淀区警方以涉嫌”非法经营罪“刑拘，现在北京市海淀区看守所关押；北京当局曾以经济问题为名调查其二人所属的出版公司，其丈夫与公司的账号均被查封；多名好友均称其被抓捕，恐与此前公开为多名中国公共知识分子及异见人士发声呼吁有关，乃是因言获罪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月遭正式逮捕。</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日遭中共当局抓捕的著名媒体人耿潇男女士因言获罪被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。后上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日二审维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日由北京市海淀区看守所转北京女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">耿宜敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，安徽省阜南县人，阜南县鹿城镇环北七路<span lang="EN-US">47</span>号公民，基督徒，安徽省阜南县基督教堂会堂主任，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，该基督教会接到当地县政府发来的欲拆除教会通知，声称政府要对阜南县富陂大道西侧实施棚改项目，而其教堂因位于该项目征收范围，所以需要拆除；因政府仅对其所在教会提出单方面拆迁补偿方案，并称若要异地重建政府将不予相应补偿，面对此单方武断决策，其及牧师、众信徒们认为明显有失公允，故遭到包括其在教会众教友的坚决反对，遂遭当局恶意报复与打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，当教堂众教友在做礼拜聚会时，突遭地方当局的强行闯入拆除，拆除时无任何合法文件及通知出示，且因事发突然，教堂财物来不及搬出，以致所有物品近都毁坏；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其与教会牧师、部分会堂成员数人被阜南县警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被阜阳县检察院予以正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在安徽省阜南县法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被该法院一审以“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；其不服，提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，安徽省阜阳市中级法院经二审裁决，认为“原判认定的部分事实不清，证据不足”，故撤销原审，发回重审。目前被羁押于阜南县女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宫文义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了宫文义等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其他<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名法轮功学员被松北区检察院起诉。宫文义因身体原因保外回家，检察院称另案处理。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，宫文义在哈尔滨市江北住处，警察再次抓捕，并被抄家。后被在哈市第一看守所关押。后宫文义于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被哈市道外区法院秘密开庭并判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被押送哈市呼兰监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">巩进军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">曾因房屋遭遇强拆而上访多年，并屡遭截访，被遣返原籍；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因长期滞留北京上访，遂被送至黑监狱马家楼关押，后又被遣返原籍，途中其一行四人（均为访民）因遭到黑保安的非人虐待且拘不让饮食，故而在其人身自由及安全被“黑保安”非法严重侵害的情况下被迫予以正当防卫，双方发生激烈冲突，引发刺死黑保安事件（警方称一死一伤）；案发后河北省饶阳县警方迅速将其抓捕刑拘，并被关押在河北省衡水市深州看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被河北省衡水市中院以“故意伤害罪”判处无期徒刑；据悉其在被审讯时曾遭严重酷刑，仅一天即被电击<span lang="EN-US">50</span>余次。目前在河北省某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡嘎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">出生年月不详，西藏自治区拉萨市林周县人，拉萨市林周县旁多乡藏民，职业不详，生态环境保护者，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早从<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年起，中国政府就开始计划将在拉萨市林周县附近的矿区建设、实施“旁多水利枢纽工程”。因该工程要在两条交汇于林周县旁多乡的河流——热振河、旁多措河之上筑坝截水，故为确保顺利开工，相关政府部门就于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年两次召开藏民大会，郑告村民此工程是“中共中央的指令，若有藏人试图阻止施工，将以政治罪名进行拘捕”。随后几年，因有关部门迅速投入大量施工准备，不仅在当地做频繁测量、建桥及建路等工作，而且炸山挖石，大量采矿，随意排放污水，导致当地的自然生态环境出现严重毁坏，附近村民的民房出现裂痕及大面积农田被毁坏等现象。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因拉萨市林周县的“旁多水利枢纽工程”正式开工，当局随立即强迫旁多乡<span lang="EN-US">119</span>户（近<span lang="EN-US">700</span>名）藏民尽快整体搬迁。因当地藏民不愿搬迁，故而多次向政府部门提出投诉请求，但均毫无果效。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，遂被迫进行集体维权与和平请愿，以期能借此阻拦破坏生态环境的采矿项目。不料却遭到中共西藏当局的强烈打压。贡嘎、白玛等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名藏族人权捍卫者因此遭拉萨市警方野蛮抓捕，自此失联。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，贡嘎、白玛等一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人案分别被拉萨市法院以“试图分裂西藏，并组织领导了以保护环境为名的抗议活动”罪由秘判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等徒刑，其亦被判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前在西藏自治区第一监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡觉尼玛（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1969</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州（以下简称阿坝州）若尔盖县人，西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺果芒学院经师，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并长期进入西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺的果芒学院对佛教进修、研读；后因曾长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成其身边主要弟子，加之自身对佛学严谨博学的治学态度，故而被哲蚌寺果芒学院确立为经师（即精通佛教经藏的僧人，又称佛教讲经诵经的师父）；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因藏区发生大规模以僧侣为主体，要求中共当局实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并呼吁让达赖喇嘛回国返乡等政治诉求的抗议活动，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其所在寺庙约有<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧人亦积极参与其中，致使抗议活动态势迅速扩展到整个拉萨市区，以及四川、青海等藏区；针对此次抗议游行，中共西藏当局很快调拨大批持枪武警，因管控手段过于极端，遂导致双方发生对峙冲突，其间有不少僧人被抓捕，其余人等被送回寺庙严管看守；尽管此前其并未参加抗议游行活动，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其仍被拉萨市警方以涉嫌“抗议活动”抓走刑拘，自此失联；另有二名哲蚌寺好友、学者僧侣亦被一同抓捕；后其被拉萨市检察院正式批捕，理由是未能阻止哲蚌寺僧人举行大规模抗议行动；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在被长期关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，被拉萨市中级法院以不详罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，据悉，其辩护权遭剥夺，其狱中具体境况等信息不明。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">贡却才培（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Kunchok Tsephel Gopey Tsang</span>，甘肃省甘南藏族自治州玛曲县欧拉乡人，曾担任玛曲县藏文中学英语教师，并任玛曲县畜牧局公务员、藏语及藏族网络作家和琼迈藏语文学网编辑，中国在押政治犯、良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年曾因涉嫌政治活动而被拘押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，后无罪获释；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年因在互联网上发表了与西藏<span lang="EN-US">3.14</span>事件有关的文章，同时向外界披露藏人在抗议事件中被镇压、军警抓捕寺院僧侣等消息，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被从家中逮捕，并遭搜查，之后与外界失去联系；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被甘肃省甘南藏族自治州中级法院秘密审判，以“泄露国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年。先在甘肃省甘南自治州合作监狱服刑，后关押地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡却卓玛（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县藏人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因手中举着达赖喇嘛尊者的法相，在县城一处街道上和平游行，以此表达自己对达赖喇嘛尊者的崇敬，随立即被驻守在街道附近的中共警方拘捕。后音信全无。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">龚月贵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，家住武穴市刊江办事处，目前被非法关押在黄冈市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄 ，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。龚月贵刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苟正琼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川泸州市法轮功学员。罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英、苟正琼，家住泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，苟正琼在泸县兆雅镇给学生讲真相时，遭兆雅镇派出所警察抓捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又在泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇，抓捕了正在各自店铺里工作的法轮功学员邓万英、雷焕英、罗太会。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，被关押了两年的泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英，苟正琼，因为信仰法轮大法，在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次庭审后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬，被泸县法院判刑：邓万英<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，雷焕英<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罗太会<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，苟正琼<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。苟正琼刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html</span></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">龚鲭林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省南充市仪陇县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，仪陇县金城镇派出所警察打电话给龚鲭林，让他把身份证拿去派出所登记一下。龚鲭林就拿着自己的身份证，去当地派出所登记，结果被警察抓捕。警察从龚鲭林身上强行搜去他家的钥匙，去他家抄家，警察非法抄走的龚鲭林的私人财物有：法轮功书籍、计算机、打印机等，现金八万多元。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，龚鲭林被庭审，并被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">龚圣亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">基督教牧师，华南教案首犯。龚圣亮牧师是湖北省枣阳市人，华南教会（<span lang="EN-US">SCC</span>）的创始人和领袖，该教派是中国一个家庭教会团契，在几个省份有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万名信徒。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，龚圣亮在湖北省钟祥市被捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，他被湖北省荆门市中级法院裁定罪名成立，根据中国的反邪教法判处死刑。但由于国际压力，中国放弃了宗教罪名和死刑，并下令重新审判。中国湖北省高级法院后以事实不清、证据不足为由驳回了荆门市中级法院对基督教华南教会五名成员的死刑判决后，荆门市中级法院重新作出一审判决，把龚圣亮、徐福明、胡勇等三人改判无期徒刑，龚邦坤、李英改判<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年有期徒刑，原先在一审被判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年徒刑的向凤屏和刘先知等四人获当庭释放。一些作证反对龚的人后来表示，他们遭到了残酷的刑讯逼供。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">古丽米拉•艾明（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1979</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区人，原任职乌鲁木齐政府机关工作人员，网络作家，中国在押政治犯、良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年因在<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>事件发生时用手机短信向境外担任挪威维吾尔协会副秘书长的丈夫拜合提亚尔联系<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多次通报看到的情况，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被新疆乌鲁木齐市警方逮捕，据称在拘留期间曾遭受酷刑虐待；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被新疆乌鲁木齐市中级人民法院以“分裂国家、泄露国家秘密和组织非法示威”罪判处无期徒刑。此前曾在乌鲁木齐水磨沟女子监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日获悉，其在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年中共新疆当局录制的认罪悔过视频中，因曾签署了一份书面忏悔声明，遂其刑期被减为<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；但因无法确认具体减刑日期，故其服刑到期日，暂不明晰；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">目前在乌鲁木齐市新疆第二监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/blog-post_99.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/blog-post_99.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">古丽仙•阿巴斯：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，新疆维吾尔自治区人，维吾尔族，退休医生，在押中国政治犯。被捕入狱前，为人生性善良、无私、正直，虽不热衷于参与政治，但有积极的奉献精神；自中共当局对新疆地区各少数族群（尤其是维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族人等）实行更严厉的高压管控以来，因其曾公开批评中共当局针对新疆维吾尔族等族群的人权不尊重、很糟糕，遂遭致新疆中共当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被新疆警方带走，自此失联；后经长达两年多的家人及国际人权组织机构连手查寻，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日终于获悉，其早被当地检察院以多项罪由予以批捕，指控其因“参与恐怖组织”、“恐怖活动”，其行为已严重地扰乱了社会秩序，故被抓捕、判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，被新疆维吾尔自治区某法院以“恐怖组织罪”、“说明恐怖活动罪”和“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。目前服刑监狱缺详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谷明龙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北保定市定州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，谷明龙因到高蓬镇钮店村发放法轮功资料被定州市公安局抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底被定州市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现被关押在唐山某监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谷秀华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区石河镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，谷秀华（女）、刘希永（男）、周兴（男）、李天学（男）、王丽志（女）、张三曼（女）、谭春荣（女）、孙宝英（女）、刘井龙（男），去大连市金普新区炮台镇袁屯村发放新书《共产主义的终极目的》，被炮台镇派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午二在大连市金州法院庭审。后谷秀华、周兴、王丽志，被大连市金州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；张三曼、谭春荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，李天学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘希永、孙宝英、刘井龙的情况还不清楚。谷秀华刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">官忠基：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省青岛市平度市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月平度市法院对法轮功学员官忠基判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，山东省青岛市法院又对官忠基上诉案维持原判。官忠基，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁，山东省平度市东阁办事处后巷子村人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，平度市七、八个警察到青岛李沧官忠基的儿子家将官忠基绑架到平度市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">桂敏海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，汉族，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日出生，原籍中国宁波，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年加入瑞典国籍，“巨流传媒有限公司”股东。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月及<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月的中共特工赴香港、泰国实施的“香港铜锣湾书店案”震惊世界，共绑架了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人，分别是桂敏海、林荣基、吕波、张志平、李波。后此<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人都于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年被中共逼迫在电视上认罪。桂敏海<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬在央视称自己是为<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年前在宁波醉驾撞死人事件而潜返中国投案自首；<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，桂敏海又在电视镜头前承认自己非法偷运禁书进入大陆。后林荣基、吕波、张志平、李波相继被释放，唯有桂敏海遭扣押。中共当局一度声称桂敏海取保获释，实际上是仍遭秘密关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被中共当局关押期间，中共称经其本人申请依法恢复中国国籍。宁波市中级法院于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日公开宣判，认定桂敏海犯为境外非法提供情报罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭成茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十四岁。郭成茹，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被天津市河西区桃园派出所警察抓捕、非法关押、构陷。这是继郭成茹过去的六次被抓捕、十二年冤狱后的第七次被抓捕。从<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日到<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日这<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年间里，即从郭成茹三十五岁到四十九岁这段日子，她两次被非法劳教、两次被非法判刑、多次被非法拘留，累计<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年时间她是被囚禁在中共的看守所、劳教所、监狱中度过的。在对法轮功的灭绝政策下，她被多次野蛮灌食迫害，被酷刑吊铐折磨，被破坏中枢神经的药物迫害到一度失忆、失语、丧失认知、表达等能力，被警察包夹折磨到一度精神失常。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份家人得知，郭成茹已被河西区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚款五千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭春该</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。目前此案音讯全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭丹霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省岳阳市石油公司退休会计、法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生。郭丹霞是于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被岳阳市楼区公安分局国保大队多个警察入室抓捕、抄家、审讯，后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被检察院批捕，六月份被关押到岳阳市康复医院（精神病医院）。后郭丹霞被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，处罚金五千元。刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭宏英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吉林省四平市铁东区人。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日是替母亲肖蕴苓、哥哥郭洪伟进京伸冤，而在“两会”期间被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天的郭宏英女士获释的日子，郭宏英的八旬老父亲拖着病体到拘留所，结果眼睁睁看着女儿被四平市铁东区分局南四纬派出所的从截走，得到的是一张由行政拘留改为刑事拘留的家属通知书。郭宏英哥哥郭洪伟原是国企中层干部，因秉公管理得罪了某同事，被其在检察院的亲属报复构陷入狱五年，因此而走上了血泪上访路。上访过程中，为了维持生计，承包了个小诊所，经营刚有起色却遭到违约，且由公安违法参与民事纠纷，造成巨大的经济损失。真是福无双至祸不单行。痛上痛冤上冤把郭洪伟几尽逼上了绝路，逐渐悟出了信访是骗局，是在用时间杀害上访人，携年迈父母进京上访遭到地方政府以敲诈政府公安罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，其<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁的老母亲也判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。郭洪伟坐着轮椅，患高危三级高血压服刑，其母肖蕴苓多病缠身高龄服刑。服刑其间母子二人多次出现病危，当局不允许保外就医，有将母子二人冤死狱中的嫌疑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉：吉林四平公民郭宏英涉嫌寻衅滋事、妨害公务案四平市铁东区法院判决书已经下达，郭宏英被以寻衅滋事罪判决<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，妨碍公务罪判决<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，执行<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: white; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭介仁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省益阳市资阳区新桥河镇新胜村村民。因土地维权持续上访要求解决村民基本医疗保障养老社保呼吁中共当局严惩新胜村村委、新桥河镇政府及益阳市资阳区区政府三级政府机构经办责任领导失职渎职、包庇纵容违法占地不法行为。郭介仁于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被益阳市公安局资阳分局刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被以涉嫌强迫交易罪的罪名批捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭平珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，家住武穴市田镇，美容院老板，目前被非法关押在蕲春县拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄 ，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，郭平珍被取保回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，郭平珍在流亡中被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。郭平珍刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭泉：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，江苏省南京市人，原南京师范大学副教授、研究生导师，中国大陆新民党创始人及代理主席，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年曾因发表公开信要求中国进行宪政改革，宣布组建“中国新民党”，主张在中国实行多党制和军队国家化等，遭受到中共当局的打压，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被南京师范大学党委以违反宪法和教师法为由撤销其副教授职务，调任数据员；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，又因撰文批评中国政府处理四川地震的方式不当而被拘押<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，再次因其在网上发表<span lang="EN-US">300</span>多篇名为《民主先声》的文章，其中涉及组成以宣传民主思想为目标的新民党，以及提出以不合作方式进行公民行动的蓝色运动倡议等内容，被南京市警方刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被江苏省宿迁市中级人民法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，刑满释放。此前在江苏省南京市浦口监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，原南京师范大学副教授、南京著名人权捍卫者郭泉因关注湖北武汉疫情，为疫区人民发声而遭中共当局抓捕，随即被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，郭泉的母亲顾潇向媒体证实，郭泉本月中旬已经被南京检察院以“涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪”批捕。南京警方指郭泉在网络上发表了国情及疫情等信息大<span lang="EN-US">500</span>篇文章，其中半数是在煽动民众。斯伟江律师<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在南京市第二看守所，会见郭泉。郭泉以煽动颠覆国家政权罪，在徐州市法院审理。对他指控，主要是微信上他的郭泉语录。郭泉满面红光，穿个短袖，身体健康。郭泉声言不惧坐牢。由徐州中院审理的郭泉煽动颠覆国家政权案，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分在南京市江宁区看守所开庭审理。郭泉的代理律师是郑州的常伯阳律师和上海的斯伟江律师。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/99.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/99.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭秀萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东聊城市法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">,2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁左右。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚，济南市铁路公安局、聊城市火车站派出所联合聊城市东昌府区国保大队、古楼派出所共十几个警察，闯入聊城市东昌府区法轮功学员华丽琴家中，把陈军、华丽琴、孙秀娥、李桂华、张亮、徐绍霞（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）和华丽琴的丈夫共<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人，抓捕到火车站派出所。火车站派出所对每位学员采指纹、勒索每人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元保证金，同时在当晚和第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天分别对<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位法轮功学员及郭秀萍等抄家，抢走了大法书、真相资料和个人财物。第二天后取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日又遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。信息来源：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/31/2021-8-31.html#zip7"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/31/2021-8-31.html#zip7</span></a></span><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">郭秀云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">北京密云区不老屯镇雁洛村人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功，自<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年到<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾先后三次被非法抓捕，其中两次被非法劳教。在劳教所，其虽受迫害，但仍坚持信仰，拒绝转化，拒写“三书”（保证书、决裂书、揭批书）。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其虽从山西省女子劳教所严管组被释放回家，但自此一直被当局视为重点“攻坚”对象，屡遭当地大队、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>、派出所、司法部门的上门骚扰、威胁、逼迫写“保证”及恐吓威胁，使其全家的正常生活受到严重干扰，家人感到巨大的压力和恐惧。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，中共开“两会”期间，郭秀云去亲友家路上，再次被不老屯派出所警方绑架，并被非法抄家，拿走电脑、打印机、法轮功真相币等私人物品，并被关押在北京市密云看守所。其关押期间，因受迫害而导致身体很差，在第一次被法庭庭审时，竟昏倒在地，家人多次要求放人遭拒。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，在没有通知家人的情况下，其被北京市密云区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭延达：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省营口市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年六十一岁。被抓捕迫害前，在市内某大酒店当过厨师，因修炼法轮功，郭延达<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被营口市站前区东桥派出所警察从家中抓捕。警察抄走郭延达家的私有财产：电脑、打印机、钱、汽车及一些物品。现在被关押在辽宁省沈阳市第一监狱第二监区。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日辽宁省营口市站前区法院对营口市法轮功学员郭延达等庭审，后得知郭延达被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> </b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭艳华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁锦州市轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生。锦州女儿河纺织厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年，郭艳华和另两位法轮功学员在发放真相资料时，遭恶意构陷，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，送马三家劳动教养院。劳教期间，郭艳华被劳役、殴打，致使其头部受到严重损伤，郭艳华劳教期满回家后，她的精神状态变得很差，时而哭，时而笑，时而高喊，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月末在家被警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月中旬，锦州市太和分局、锦州市太和区检察院、锦州市太和区法院沆瀣一气，判郭艳华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年刑期，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">果然： </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，北京市朝阳区人，陕西省西安市南郊大学城自由生意人，政治异见人士，中国在押政治犯。近年来，因与友人经常在自己生意所在地聚会，自由讨论追求自由民主途径，被中共当局跟踪知晓，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年二人被西安市长安区警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”抓捕刑拘，关押在西安市南郊三爻村看守所；之后因当局控其欲与他人密谋推翻中共政府，被西安市警方转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案被陕西省西安市中级法院庭审，终被以“颠覆国家政权罪”一审重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；另一人士亦被重判，但缺详情；据悉，因其平素做事隐秘，而当局对其审判亦不公开，故而对其入狱详情几乎鲜为人知，直至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日陕西省渭南市中级法院在网上发布了一份“果然减刑刑事裁决书”才得知晓，渭南监狱鉴于其在狱中有悔过表现，积分较多，建议减刑，但渭南市中级法院却以“屡次严重违反监规被处分”为由拒不减刑，依旧刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。目前在陕西省渭南监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">H.</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><o:p></o:p></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈布力（哈萨克）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">哈哈尔麦<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿合曼（</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈萨克）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">胡勇、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">胡友刚、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡玉兰</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、胡占亭、胡志琴、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">华丽琴</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄彪、黄春玲、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄建民、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄金桔、黄俊娟、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">黄敏</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、黄琦、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄日新、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黄晓敏、</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">黄醒民</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄秀兰、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄雪琴</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、黄云敏、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄治萍</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">哈布力（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐县人，哈萨克族，穆斯林，新疆乌鲁木齐县哈萨克族清真寺阿訇（即伊斯兰宗教事务主持人），伊斯兰宗教领袖。因近来中共当局加强了对新疆各民族在宗教信仰上的高压管控手段，哈萨克族人也不例外，此间，因哈布力是乌鲁木齐县哈萨克族群中知名宗教界领袖，影响力大，并与海外宗教性事务多有交流联系，随遭地方当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年被乌鲁木齐县警方抓捕，后被乌鲁木齐县检察院正式批捕，控其“阅读及复印哈萨克斯坦国家宗教事务局的刊物”，违反了国家宗教问题的相关规定；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年被新疆乌鲁木齐县法院以不具名罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。据悉，当局对其如此重判是为了震慑新疆的哈萨克族人。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈哈尔麦<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿合曼：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，新疆塔城沙湾县人，哈萨克族，塔城地区托里县托里镇复兴路小区居民，前塔城地区东湾镇民族中学校长，前塔城地区沙湾县畜牧局党委书记，原塔城地区沙湾县宗教事务办公室领导，原塔城地区沙湾县第二中学校长，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于新疆塔城师范学院中专，<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月毕业后又在新疆教育学院政治系进修大专，并于<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年毕业；曾常年在民族学校历任校长，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月曾任新疆塔城地区东湾镇民族中学校长，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年至被捕前，曾长期担任塔城地区沙湾县第二中学校长等；因工作敬业、成绩斐然，曾被当地政府多次评为“先进个人”<span lang="EN-US">/</span>“双文明先进个人”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，被沙湾县警方突然带走，并被送某教育集中营接受“政治再教育”；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">后被转为正式逮捕，指控其在工作期间因严重违反法律和违反党纪，并在宗教事务办公室期间签署建造清真寺的合同，有贿赂之嫌，所以应予逮捕判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，知其已在同年早些时候被新疆塔城地区法院以“违反党纪国法罪”和“受贿罪”秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日获悉，沙湾县中共纪律检查委员会（简称“纪检委”）曾向其家属明确表示，如要让其释放，必须交纳保释金<span lang="EN-US">40</span>万元人民币，后其家人实际交保<span lang="EN-US">80</span>万元，故其最终被执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月；另据悉，其在被判刑前曾被迫认罪，身体极差，家属被软禁，探视权被剥夺。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区乌苏监狱（新疆维吾尔自治区塔城地区乌苏监狱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">833006</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/19.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/19.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈里斯别克·巴班（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1987</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区昌吉回族自治州呼图壁县人，哈萨克族，新疆乌鲁木齐市居民，哈萨克民歌手，中国在押良心犯。身为一哈萨克族歌手，因喜欢传唱民族歌曲而深受亲友及当地民众的好评；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因曾到昌吉州吉木萨尔县泉子街镇吾塘沟村<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号参加表演，在表演会上演唱了“得罪中共当局”的歌曲，随遭到中共新疆当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，被乌鲁木齐市警方以涉嫌“宣扬非法宗教等罪”抓捕，并被指控唱了政府认为“不该唱的歌曲”；据悉，自被捕后一直失联，家属不知其具体案情，只知至今尚未判刑，但又不被释放。目前被羁押于呼图壁县监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈木拉提<span lang="EN-US">.</span>吾甫尔</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：男，维吾尔族，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月出生，研究生医学博士，“国家长江学者创新团队发展计划”发起者，曾任“新疆医科大学校长”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年曾入选中国科学院院士曾选初步候选人名单，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月任新疆食药监局局长。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，最后一次在媒体上露面。现被证实，已被乌鲁木齐警方以“传播极端民族主义思想”罪由被抓，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span
